<user>111772497277292532382<//user><time>1620877715281< /time>< Review>
J Wilds is basically a bar + barbecue. I tried one of their specialty drinks which is a Smoking Fashioned. It is delivered in a Mason jar with a lid. Inside the jar is a very good old fashioned & a big puff of apple wood smoke. Significant effect on the flavor of the drink.
Our appetizer was grilled brussel sprouts w/ bacon, onions,& vinegar reduction. These are also avail as a side.
I had brisket, choice of 2 lean, or 2 fatty, or 1+1. I had cornbread & Mac & Cheese. My husband had 1/2 chicken with Cole slaw & biscuit. I thought cornbread was better than biscuit. There are 5 different barbecue sauces to put on the meat. Dessert was very good: cake or cobbler.
Place was very busy, staff was rushed but attentive & reliable. A tasty & pleasant meal.</Review>

<time>1615229906846< /time><Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
I don‚Äôt usually leave reviews but I thought J Wilds was deserving of one last night!

We ordered the 3x3 for take out - pulled pork, ribs, brisket, Mac and cheese, sprouts, wild fries and the corn bread and giant biscuit. I got home and realized we were missing the pulled pork and cornbread. Normally, I would let it slide and not even call, but we were excited for the pulled pork - plus we did pay quite a bit extra for the additional meat. So I called and was immediately greeted with apologies and options of a refund or a remake. I opted for the remake and luckily I live close enough that I was able to be there in 10 minutes. I was again greeted with apologies and the man I spoke with offered to throw in a few orders of their whiskey cake and ice cream for the inconvenience. I was thrilled to have such a great experience and seeing them truly take care of their customers! I wish I remembered the names of the employees I spoke with, all of them were all great as well!

The food was absolutely phenomenal! We bbq and smoke our own ribs, pork and brisket frequently so we know good bbq. The sides were great as well! We will absolutely be back!< /Text>

<rating>5</rating>< Review>
I had heard of Barry's but I thought is it really worth the $$ and the hype? Oh yes it is!! I'm not someone who likes to spend money on expensive boutique/bougie places unless they are worth it and Barry's is just that. I went to my first class and a wonderful front staff showed me around the small studio. He clearly explained what things were and where everything was. I felt somewhat comfortable before class started and definitely not intimidated by all the pros in the class. My neighbors fist-bumped me and it was great. The workout itself is AMAZING. I was sore for days after and my heart was pumping and I was drenched in sweat. I'm not a great runner but the threadmill sprinting intervals were so much fun. The floor exercises were also powerful and the instructor went around the room to make sure we were all doing it correctly. Best part- I could actually hear the instructor and the music wasn't too loud. The lights even helped getting the running off my mind. I honestly can't wait to go back and Barry's... just take my money!</Review>

< text>
While the price is extremely high for a workout, the workout I admit is quite good. You will almost always leave sore if you follow the instructor's commands. By running with inclines of 8-10% along with 8-11MPH runs, you are guaranteed to run out breath.

It is a great workout for the full body. If you are looking for concentrated workouts like bodybuilding or cardio, you could do that yourself at the gym at your own pace. If you are looking to do a combination without knowing how to structure a workout, Barry's is a good alternative.<//text>

Barry's Bootcamp workouts are hardcore and intense. You will break a sweat and have a good time doing it. My favorite instructors are Chris R. Tommy L. and Gabby. <time>1412710826335<//time><rating>4< /rating>< Review>
If you want a cardio + some strength training class, then you're set!

I really wanted to LOVE Barry's, but I just like it.  If just came back from a vacation, or if you just need to get back into working out, Barry's is a great class to take.  BUT if you're looking to increase strength, I wouldn't do this class.

They do have a strength portion to every workout, but it's all about reps and you don't really get to isolate or do as many sets as you would like.  For instance, for Butts and Legs day, I did two sets of strength training for butts, but it was a different exercise.  We would spend maybe 1 minute on each exercise and that was it.  Not great for strength.<//Review>

<Name>Sylvia Lewis<//Name><pics>None< /pics>< text>
Pros: Excellent workout, motivating instructors. Also the smoothies looked great (next time I go, I'll get one).

Cons: It's filled to the brim with Marina types. There will be copious bros and blonde... bro-ettes(?). There will be grunting by the bros. There will be whoos and yeahs! by the girls. But the music and your heart will be thumping so it's easy to ignore.

Also just to clarify for those that are anxious about this class - I'm not a fantastic runner (I get winded at 6 mph at 10 minutes on the treadmill at 1% incline) and felt an unreasonable level of anxiety about this class due to the previous reviews. I had this incorrect misconception that you would be sprinting at 9 mph at various inclines for the entire 10 minutes on the treadmill. Instead, the treadmill portion is VERY interval based. You will be recovering a lot (walking or jogging - typically at an incline) and then sprinting for typically tens of seconds. It's challenging but it won't kill you or make you hurl. For reference: I started working out approximately a month ago so I'm fit but not in athlete shape.

So don't worry and give it a try!< /text>

<review>Just took my first Barry's class this past weekend and I don't think I'm exaggerating when I say it was the toughest workout of my life. I have never sweated or pushed myself that hard before and everyone left the class completely drenhed. The crazy thing was that I wasn't actually that sore the next day (I think it was due to all the cardio??) but it really was a full body workout.

The setup of the class is about 40 people split into two groups: treadmills and weights and you switch groups a couple of times to make sure you are really going as hard as you can at each segment. The room is dark and the music is loud but it really allowed me to lose myself for the hour I was there. It was such an exhilarating experience!  I definitely took a nap after that but was OK to workout the next day. Highly recommend Barrys - I'll be back!< /review>< Pictures>

< Text>
Our family is from san Francisco and my brother in law is from Turlock. I love giving him a hard time about the fact there aren‚Äôt enough great places in Turlock. Well, Bistro 234 has something to say about that.

We ordered a few appetizers and the bacon wrapped scallops were eaten before I could take a picture. There was a nice crunch on the bacon and the scallops were nice and soft inside. Very flavorful and very juicy.

I like measuring a higher end restaurant by how they make their burger and this did not disappoint. The meat was amazing and the fries were spot on, super crispy and well seasoned. Think crunchy gourmet In and Out fries.

The belle of the ball was the lamb shank. The lamb was extremely juicy, full of flavor and was shared amongst the table because it was amazing. It was a special of the day and not on the regular menu.

The table also ordered the gnocchi, NY strip and the Mahi Mahi which were all Good but not memorable.

The service here was great. The waitress was attentive and helpful and the manager graciously  resolved a small issue for us on the wine.

I would recommend this place for a nice dinner in downtown Turlock. The food and service were great.< /Text>

< review>
I was so looking forward to going here, but was underwhelmed. We took staff here for a company Christmas dinner, because we wanted to offer them something nice. Our table was right by the entrance next to the bar so there was lots of traffic. Service was very slow because our waiter was serving another large table. Food presentation of appetizers was good and they were tasty. Food presentation for main courses was really non existent. Dinner bowl with meat, potato and veggie. Like I do at home for the family. They had a special of rack of lamb that was prepared really well, but served in a dinner bowl. Try cutting a lamb chop in a bowl in a confined space ... you might end up wearing it. I suggest a flat dinner plate for this type of dish. Dessert presentation was average. All in all we were underwhelmed and will not rush back.</review>

<name>Gregory Gonzales<//name><date>1514529931984</date><Rating>2</Rating>< review>
The clams are awesome, sweet, spicy, garlicy, buttery; if you go you should try them. However, my wife's Chicken Marsala dish; the filets flaked apart like a fish!!! Never seen it before in that dish. It means the chicken was braised for an awful long time not sauteed; furthermore, the mushrooms may have been dehydrated from their appearance, thin tough, texture of leather. This was a poorly executed dish. 234 gained noteriety from that dish yet it was less to be desired today and for 23 bucks an utter disappointment. Chilean Sea Bass was very good, cooked perfectly, tarragon aoli was tartar sauce with little to no tarragon to taste. Lastly, the Jasmine rice; it might as be mom's rice pudding from left over rice, great dessert but not for dinner entree accompaniment. Wait service could not or would not reflect upon the chicken impression demonstration I provided her. Disappointed customer.</review>

<gmapID>0x8091064bce8f40c9:0x4d61058bb6e0ec3<//gmapID><Name>Lucas Triffo<//Name>< rating>
2<//rating>
< review>
TLDR: Subpar service and nothing special about the food. Pick a different place for lunch if you are already in downtown Turlock.
Context:
Went to celebrate my sister graduating college. We had a party of five.we arrived for lunch and had a reservation for noonish. The restaurant was not busy, though they may have had a party in the backroom.
Service: 1/5
Slow and largely absent for the majority of the meal. We were seated at 12-ish and we're not able to place our food order until at least 12:30. The sandwiches we ordered took 45-60 minutes to arrive. Normally if the quality is great, that doesn't bug me, but what we received was rather subpar for the price. When we asked for something on the side with the meal (after it was delivered), we never got it. Our waiter did not come to check on us, and stopped by at 1:30/2 to see if we wanted dessert. We asked what the options were and told him we needed a moment to decide. We never saw him again until he dropped off the bill (after we paid) luckily the hostess came by 20 minutes later and was able to take our dessert order, bring the desserts, and find a different waiter to bring out our bill.
Food: 2/5
All the food options were plain. Like, white people that can't handle seasoning plain. The burger we ordered (there was only 1 on the menu) came with nothing but cheese on it. When we asked, a waiter (not ours) told us the other burger had lots of stuff, but the one we must have ordered comes plain. Again, there was only one burger option on the menu. One of our other people ordered his sandwich with a salad and got fries, the fries I received were room temperature at best and way saltier than everyone else's.
Atmosphere: 4/5
Pretty restaurant, great location. There really is a lot of potential here to be a great place.< /review>

< Review>
I am here from Los Angeles on a visit and wanted to try some local pizza. I looked around and found this spot. They only have outside seating which works for me because we take our dog everywhere. The owner was super friendly and made great conversation. All in all the atmosphere, the food and the people really sold this place.

Now the food... The food was great. I had a simple pepperoni pizza. I feel a pepperoni pizza is a good place to start when trying a pizza place. They use a nice fatty pepperoni that has a good amount of grease to it but doesn't leave your mouth feeling oily. They use a good mozzarella and their sauce is slightly thick and on the sweeter side. The crust is on the thinner side but with a good bready chew. All in all, it was a great pizza.

My only regret was that I discovered they had baked sandwiches, not too different from a calzone, after eating 3/4th of my pizza. I forget the name of the sandwiches but I'm sure there's an image of the menu.

This place gets my 5 stars. I highly recommend coming here. This place is a prime example of why people shop local/small business.< /Review>

My favorite fish store in town. Why?  Recently got back into the hobby with a 30 gallon clear for life, I needed to stock it. Luckily the "Dragon" helped select the right ones for me. I really wanted a pair of Oscars and a convict, but after conversation of what i am looking for , got  5 other smaller cichlids that suited my needs. I am glad he was so helpful. Prices are great, always willing to make a deal. I like this store because the owner is so friendly and customer oriented. may be a week or a year since you go, but he will still remember you. Great people, it's worth checking out for all you fresh water, cichlid african/south american, etc.. or just need a replacement pump or a quick batch of meds, etc..  lots of other medium sized fish to stock your large aquarium or storefront. Call ahead for salt/ live rock  and other options avail.Customer service A+.  Worth stopping by.</review>

< text>
My son is graduating this year after four years of an absolutely outstanding experience. Their high level of education; care, attention, support and understanding is nothing less than excellent. Add to that the conservatories that provide a cultural education and appreciation for the arts and you have a formula that is unmatched and invaluable. Yes, it is not easy to get in, students need both an academic and arts proficiency, but it is well worth a try. Students graduate and move on to top-rated colleges and universities, with the added value of an otherwise costly and rare opportunity to grow in their chosen art field.< /text>

<Pics>None</Pics>< review>
OCSA is not your normal high school experience. It's unique in the fact that it is a very welcoming community for LGBT+ and all sorts of artistic people. I've met amazing people here, but I will be transferring out due to the 9 1/2 hour day schedule and other personal reasons. Unfortunately, there is only a few categories in which certain people are not as accepted as others. A straight, white, religious student at OCSA faces a surprising amount of playful jokes, but we all know how often "playful jokes" are considered funny. A great school for a lot of kids, but just not right for other kinds. :)<//review>

< username>
Susan Golian</username>
< Review>
It is said that Disneyland is the happiest place on earth - I disagree - I believe OCSA deserves that moniker. Middle school and high school can be horrible, but the staff and students at OCSA make the school a wonderful, fun, joyous experience. Except for a couple of teachers who were duds (and most of them didn't last more than a year), the teachers are fantastic - they WANT to be at OCSA because the students are motivated and engaged.

And then there's just the wild creativity - best day of the year is Halloween - hands down! The costumes the kids come up with are simply amazing (my all-time fave? the boy who wore a sheet with empty candy boxes, popcorn and empty soda cups stuck to it and a popcorn container on his head like a crown - he was the floor of the movie theater after the show!!!).

The principal and vice-principal, as well as the campus security, deserve special mention for making the school safe, keeping the kids just disciplined enough to keep them out of trouble but not so tight that their creativity is squelched, and for listening sensitively and acting immediately when there's any sort of problem. All in all, OCSA is the best school I've ever been exposed to - I am so incredibly grateful that my daughter spent 6 years there.< /Review>

<Text>Good, fresh-tasting and well-prepared fish and sides. Both the grilled and fried fish were great. The catfish, corn side and slaw were particularly good. Their self service soda station has mostly gourmet sodas. There's a fairly large condiment bar with homemade ketchup, salsa and tarter sauce and a lot more. The prices are low for the quality of food. The cashier service was helpful and polite. The food took awhile to be prepared, but the place was pretty busy while I was there. It has a clean, pleasant, modern interior with outdoor seating in front. They also sell beer and wine. Most meals come with a choice of 2 side dishes. Note that there are house sides and premium sides, which can be selected for a added charge. The roasted street corn is premium, though worth the extra charge.< /Text>< Pictures>

I ordered the Dynamite Shrimp Bowl. It was amazing! My wife had the breaded calamari which she found to be just okay. The portions are large and the price is fair for what you receive. The ingredients options are definitely on the healthier side. Definitely will come by again to try their other offerings.

A salmon dish may have been a better choice for me personally. I did like their dynamite sauce on the Rockfish and fries. The sauce has a nice kick. I would definitely come back again and try new dishes!<//Text>

<Rate>3<//Rate>< review>
There's a lot to like about this establishment.  The place is clean and well organized, the staff are friendly and in some cases enthusiastic, and I always like outdoor seating.

However, the downside is that the location is not great and the food is 'uninspired'.  Given that the ingredient quality seems to be high-medium, I expected it to taste great, but everything that I tried was bland or one-dimensional.  I think that the staff and cooks are doing a fine job, but the recipes need to be reworked.  Even the salsa is boring.  As someone who has eaten a lot of shrimp tacos, I always thought that it was impossible to make wrong.  I now know differently.< /review>

<Date>1487617084220< /Date><rating>5<//rating>< text>
The chef at Tanaka takes pride in every dish he presents. Each dish is beautifully presented on white plates which gives focuses the presentation on the fish.  The fish is extraordinarily fresh and the chef highlights each piece with different salts, fresh yuzu, fresh wasabi, and light citrus sauces. I recommend the omakase... And for this kind of quality at this price you can't find anywhere. The service is very pleasant and attentive. Never intrusive but always aware of the tables and your needs. If you are looking for soy sauce and special rolls go else where. But if you are looking for artisticly presented, fresh fish in a quiet, low key setting I highly recommend Tanaka Sushi.<//text>

<userid>104874990698766503329< /userid><name>Chester Lin</name><Date>1512714721206<//Date><rate>5</rate><text>Words cannot describe how good the sushi is here. You'll be amazed and puzzled. You'll find yourself asking... Am I really in a Simi valley strip mall? What is this fish? Where does one get it? Gingko fish, sea robin...

<rating>5</rating><gmapID>0x80e829aa1fc9d8b3:0xe18c7bc061f759c5</gmapID>< Review>
I mean, wow. If you want some of the highest quality, traditional style sushi straight from Japan, this is the place to come. I travel all around looking for the freshest fish and authentic style of serving sushi and this check marks every box. The chef is from Japan and clearly has been trained in the art of fine sushi. His fish is top notch , the service is impeccable and the level of detail he put to each piece of nigiri is exceptional. Don't expect stupid saucy Americanized rolls and soy sauce platters to drench rolls into. He glazes each fish with its own sauce to compliment that specific fish. It's a small little place, very clean and organized. Let the chef do his thing and take his omakase course if your new to this type of sushi. Otherwise go down that nigiri list and enjoy yourself. This place is a hidden gem and I will definitely be going back soon.<//Review>

<GmapID>0x80e829aa1fc9d8b3:0xe18c7bc061f759c5<//GmapID><Time>1477974935603<//Time>< user_id>

<rate>5</rate><Review>I love this place. So, I left this same lengthy review on Yelp. This has to be the rarest gem in Simi Valley. If you are looking for authentic sushi and outstanding service, this is the place to be. The restaurant itself is situated next to a hair salon and doesn't look anything out of the ordinary from the outside. Don't be fooled! The inside was elegant, quiet, charming, and very clean. We sat at the bar and ordered the $100 Omakase meal per person. Totally worth every penny and all 15 dishes. The sushi chef had exemplary skills and attention to detail. Each dish we ordered was so delicious and presented so well. You can tell that he had knife skills with the precision he had with the cuts on the fish and how he prepared everything.

You must drink with sake when you come here,  it will make your dinner even more enjoyable. The vibe was very relaxing in the restaurant. Limited seating so it's best to make reservations in advance.

I came here for my birthday on October 14 and I was shocked when the lovely waitress came up next to me with a sweet "Happy Birthday!" and handed me a plate of what I believe were the best tasting ice cream mochi Ive had by far. And I have had a lot of Mochi Ice cream before . Most Japanese restaurants seem to just serve the store bought ones. This, however, was the real deal. The mochi dough was melt-in-your-mouth delicious! The vanilla ice cream inside was so smooth and creamy, almost as if they just made it. They even added a birthday candle on one. I wasn't expecting that since I dont think I've ever had a birthday mochi before. It was so simple and perfect.

All I have left to say is, DEFINITELY give this place a try because it's totally worth checking out.

I will be coming back for sure.</Review>< Pictures>
